posted:Posted May 3, 2024
msg:The hotel is located in Xinghai Bay, with a unique harbor location. It takes about ten minutes to walk from the hotel to the A2 entrance of Xinghai Square Metro Station. The hotel faces the Xinghai Bay Bridge and the seaside. The rooms are elegantly decorated and comfortable and spacious. Every staff member of the hotel is very polite and enthusiastic. When checking in, the front desk receptionist Wang Xin Allen was very kind and friendly. He also gave me an upgrade in the room type. The room is clean and tidy, with floor-to-ceiling glass windows to enjoy the vast sea view of Xinghai Bay and the light show of Xinghai Bay Bridge at night. The hotel and the guest rooms provide free Wi-Fi. There is a comfortable big bed and automatic curtains in the room. The washing area is separated into dry and wet areas, and the induction smart toilet is fully equipped... The shower area also has a large bathtub and Balmain brand toiletries, which are really easy to use. The room service also cleans very clean every day. There is a fitness room and an indoor swimming pool on the 4th floor of the hotel. I stayed at the Grand Hyatt for 5 days and 4 nights. Overall, it is highly recommended!

One of the plans is to go to the zoo. It takes more than 10 minutes to drive, which is super convenient!
The second plan is to ride a multi-person bicycle at Xinghai Square. Just go downstairs. Don't be too happy. You don't need to think about parking. Perfect!
About the meal:
There are a lot of breakfast items, but they are actually not five-star, more like a canteen, especially the coffee shop! It can be used as a feeling of collective life! The dinner buffet looked at the food and there was no choice. The Hui family of ours is really limited!
About living:
We are a deluxe double room, the bed is a little smaller, and the decoration is online for hotels that have been around for nearly ten years! The pillows are not friendly, bring your own for babies with bad cervical spine!
About service:
The aunt on the floor was very touched by the joyful Good Morning daughter. The front desk was considerate when checking out. The elevator in the parking lot was not easy to use. Call the front desk to deal with it in time and sincerely apologize. The parking will automatically bind the check-in date to any entry and exit, which is very convenient! There are no other special services. Compared with the current "Haidilao"-style hotel services, it is a bit more relaxed.
On the whole, it is worth buying back, and the overall experience is better than the castle hotel I lived in before!
